<ul>
<li>This property is only returned for ERA enrollments in <code>LIVE</code> status with at least one matching ERA from the payer.</li>
<li>If this timestamp doesn&#x27;t match your expected timeline for ERA processing, there may be an upstream issue. Contact Stedi support for assistance.</li>

class="px-2.5 py-1 rounded-md font-[500] text-[13px] bg-transparent ring-1 ring-inset ring-neutral-300 dark:ring-neutral-700 text-neutral-700 dark:text-neutral-300 break-all">Length:<!-- --> <!-- -->5 - 10</span></div></div><div class="prose-no-margin pt-4 pb-4 empty:hidden text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>This property is required for payers that require a Provider Transaction Access Number (PTAN).</p>
<p>The PTAN is a Medicare-issued number given to providers upon enrollment with Medicare. This number is usually six digits and is assigned based on the type of service and the location of the provider. Upon enrollment, Medicare Administrating Contracting (MAC) providers should receive their assigned PTAN number in their approval letter.</p></div></div><div class="text-sm border-t openapi-property -->8</span></div></div><div class="prose-no-margin pt-4 pb-4 empty:hidden text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>The requested effective date for the enrollment in YYYYMMDD format. This is the date the enrollment is requested to take effect with the payer. If not provided during submission, Stedi uses the submission date.</p>
<p>Stedi can&#x27;t guarantee that the enrollment will be effective with the payer on this exact date. Not all payers support future dates. If the payer supports a requested effective date, Stedi will process enrollments accordingly.</p></div></div><div class="text-sm border-t openapi-property scroll-mt-32 w-full href="#response.status" lang="en" style="word-break:break-word;overflow-wrap:break-word;hyphens:auto;-webkit-hyphens:auto;-ms-hyphens:auto"><span class="inline-flex items-center gap-1 min-w-0" 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span></span></a><div class="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-1 mt-3"><span class="px-2.5 py-1 rounded-md font-[500] text-[13px] bg-blue-50 dark:bg-blue-950/50 text-blue-700 dark:text-blue-300 break-all whitespace-normal inline-flex items-center gap-1"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon size-3.5"><path d="M3 4H21V6H3V4ZM3 19H17V21H3V19ZM3 14H21V16H3V14ZM3 9H17V11H3V9Z"></path></svg>String</span></div></div><div class="prose-no-margin pt-4 pb-4 empty:hidden text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>The status of the enrollment. You can submit enrollments with either <code>DRAFT</code> or <code>STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED</code> status. The default status is <code>DRAFT</code> if not specified. When you&#x27;re ready for Stedi to begin processing the enrollment, set the status to <code>STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED</code>. Once an enrollment is <code>STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED</code>, only Stedi can set or update its status.</p>
<ul>
<li><code>DRAFT</code> - You&#x27;re still editing the enrollment and haven&#x27;t submitted it to Stedi.</li>
<li><code>STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED</code> - You have submitted the enrollment and it is ready for Stedi to begin processing.</li>
<li><code>PROVIDER_ACTION_REQUIRED</code> - The enrollment requires action from the healthcare provider to proceed, such as providing additional documentation. Stedi will add a note to your enrollment request with clear instructions.</li>
<li><code>SUBMITTED</code> - (Deprecated) Legacy status being phased out in favor of the more specific action-required statuses. If you set an enrollment request to <code>SUBMITTED</code>, Stedi treats it as <code>STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED</code>.</li>
<li><code>PROVISIONING</code> - Stedi has begun the process of completing the enrollment with the payer.</li>
<li><code>LIVE</code> - The enrollment process is complete, and the specified provider can begin exchanging the listed transaction types with the payer.</li>
<li><code>REJECTED</code> - The payer rejected the enrollment. Common reasons for rejection include incorrect details in the request and that the provider is not credentialed with the payer. Customer support will contact you with reasons for rejection and next steps.</li>
<li><code>CANCELED</code> - The enrollment has been terminated per customer or provider request.</li>
</ul><div><section class="rounded-md border bg-fd-card"><div class="flex flex-wrap justify-between p-3 border-t border-b first:border-t-0 last:rounded-b-md first:rounded-t-md"><div aria-level="1" bg-transparent ring-1 ring-inset ring-neutral-300 dark:ring-neutral-700 text-neutral-700 dark:text-neutral-300 break-all">Format: <!-- -->date-time</span></div></div><div class="prose-no-margin pt-4 pb-4 empty:hidden text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>The date and time when the enrollment status was last updated. This timestamp is used to track enrollment processing durations and enables filtering to identify recently changed enrollments. It automatically updates whenever an enrollment&#x27;s status changes but remains unchanged during other updates.</p></div></div><div class="text-sm border-t openapi-property scroll-mt-32 w-full submitted. If the enrollment is in <code>DRAFT</code> status, <code>submittedAt</code> is not present. You can submit enrollments with either `DRAFT` or `STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED` status. The default status is `DRAFT` if not specified. When you're ready for Stedi to begin processing the enrollment, set the status to `STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED`. Once an enrollment is `STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED`, only Stedi can set or update its status.\n  - `DRAFT` - You're still editing the enrollment and haven't submitted it to Stedi.\n  - `STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED` - You have submitted the enrollment and it is ready for Stedi to begin processing.\n  - `PROVIDER_ACTION_REQUIRED` - The enrollment requires action from the healthcare provider to proceed, such as providing additional documentation. Stedi will add a note to your enrollment request with clear instructions.\n  - `SUBMITTED` - (Deprecated) Legacy status being phased out in favor of the more specific action-required statuses. If you set an enrollment request to `SUBMITTED`, Stedi treats it as `STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED`.\n  - `PROVISIONING` - Stedi has begun the process of completing the enrollment with the payer.\n  - `LIVE` - The enrollment process is complete, and the specified provider can begin exchanging the listed transaction types with the payer.\n  - `REJECTED` - The payer rejected the enrollment. Common reasons for rejection include incorrect details in the request and that the provider is not credentialed with the payer. Customer support will contact you with reasons for rejection and next steps.\n  - `CANCELED` - The enrollment has been terminated per customer or provider
